# Shops | EconomyShopGUI wiki

The file name defines the shop internal name and needs to match the filename for the [section](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/sections.yml)
 config inside the sections folder

[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#general-information-about-the-shops-configuration)

General information about the shops configuration.


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Since version v6 or Premium v5 of the plugin, sections are stored in their seperate config, instead of using a single sections.yml config to store all of them.

These configs store all items for the specific shop category(section) which are linked to the specific sections config. This config stores all contents of the shop including shop items and per page configurations.

*   Custom items from other plugins are only supported with ESGUI-Premium. (Unless they are created with keys available in the Free version)
    

We recommend you change the prices of the items to suit your server's economy. There are many different types of servers, such as skyblock, survival, factions, pvp, etc... Most servers will need to customize the shops to their needs and have different prices from other servers. If you choose to use the default configs as-is, you may. You may also check [discord #Shop-Files-Sharing](https://discord.com/invite/nPyuB4F)
 channel for shop files that may suit your needs.

[Please read About YAML](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/about-yaml-yml-files)
 before editing your files! It DOES NOT tolerate any errors! [Validate it!](https://jsonformatter.org/yaml-validator)

*   TIP: Use the contents on the right side of this page to navigate quickly!
    

#### 

[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#file-format-structure)

File format structure:

Copy

    ###### code formatting reference names: ######
    pages:
      <page>:
        items:
          <itemIndex>:
            <key>: <value> #Single value key
            <key>: #List-format must support multiple values. (lore, enchants, etc..)
            - <value1>
            - <value2>
    ###### example: ######
    pages:
      page1:
        gui-rows: 6
        title: "&dCustom title for this page"
        items:
          item1:
            material: PAPER
            name: "Egyptian Papyrus"
            buy: 6
            sell: 2
            lore:
            - "Papyrus from ancinet Egypt"

[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#item-settings)

Item settings/keys:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#item-keys-list)

Item keys list:

*   [**material:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#material)
     - The item type (the [block ID or Name\_spaced name](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/item_id_list_pc.php)
     given to it by Mojang)
    
*   [**buy:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#buy)
     - Price the item will cost to purchase.
    
*   [**sell:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#sell)
     - Price the item is worth when sold to the shop/server.
    
*   [**name:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#name)
     - The name of the item
    
*   [**displayname:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#display-name)
     \- The name shown on the item _**in the shop only**_, it is NOT applied to the given item
    
*   [**lore:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#lore)
     - a list of custom text applied to the item.
    
*   [**displaylore:**](https://gpplugins.gitbook.io/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#displaylore-optional-any-item)
     _-_ a list of custom text applied to _**the shop item only**_, it is NOT applied to the given item.
    
*   [**hidePricingLore:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#hidepricinglore-optional-any-item)
     - hide the default pricing lore for the item
    
*   [hideDecorationLore:](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#hidepricinglore)
     - hide the usage/decoration lore per item
    
*   [**slot:**](https://gpplugins.gitbook.io/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#slot-optional-any-item)
     - This option is used to determine the slot inside the shop section
    
*   [**stack-size:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#stack-size)
     - This option adds a custom stack size to the item
    
*   [**enchantment-glint:**](https://gpplugins.gitbook.io/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#enchantment-glint-optional)
     - This option lets u use a enchantment effect on the item.
    
*   [**enchantments:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#enchantments)
     - a list of enchantments and level.
    
*   [**potiontypes:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#potion-types)
     - a list of potion types
    
*   [**spawnertype:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#spawner-type)
     - the mob that a spawner is set to by ESGUI when placed. \[ONLY for `spawner` material/item.\
    \
*   [**recipes:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#recipie)\
     - the recipe(s) that a `knowledge_book` will give when used\
    \
*   [**skullowner:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#skull-owner)\
     - the texture or player's skull that will be displayed by the `player_head` item.\
    \
*   [**armorcolor:**](https://gpplugins.gitbook.io/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#armor-color-required-specific-item-any-leather-armor-piece)\
     \- the rgb color of a leather armor piece.\
    \
*   [**duration:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#duration-colors-fade-colors-flicker-trail-shape-required-specific-item-firework)\
    , [**colors:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#duration-colors-fade-colors-flicker-trail-shape-required-specific-item-firework)\
    , [**fade-colors:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#duration-colors-fade-colors-flicker-trail-shape-required-specific-item-firework)\
    , [**flicker:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#duration-colors-fade-colors-flicker-trail-shape-required-specific-item-firework)\
    , [**trail:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#duration-colors-fade-colors-flicker-trail-shape-required-specific-item-firework)\
    , [**shape:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#duration-colors-fade-colors-flicker-trail-shape-required-specific-item-firework)\
     - these options can be used to create a firework\
    \
*   [**instrument:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#undefined)\
     - Specifies the sound effect that comes from a Goat Horn\
    \
*   [**section:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#sub-sections)\
     \- Links the item to a shop section\
    \
*   [**stew-effect:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#stew-effect)\
     - Gives a specific effect to a suspicious stew\
    \
*   [**armor-trim:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#armor-trim)\
     Sets a armor trim to a armor piece\
    \
*   [**hidden:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#hidden)\
     - Hides the item from the GUI but can still be sold to shop\
    \
*   [**max-buy:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#max-buy)\
     - Sets the maximum amount of items which can be bought per transaction\
    \
*   [**max-sell:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#max-sell)\
     - Sets the maximum amount of items which can be sold per transaction\
    \
*   [**min-buy:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#min-buy)\
     \- Sets the minimum amount of items which is required to be bought per transaction\
    \
*   [**min-sell:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#min-sell)\
     - Sets the minimum amount of items which is required to be sold per transaction\
    \
*   [**prior-lore:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#prior-lore)\
     \- Whether or not to prioritize default pricing lore\
    \
*   [**close-menu:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#close-menu)\
     \- Whether or not to close the shop GUI after a transaction has been made\
    \
*   [**display-item:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#display-items)\
     - Can be used to create a different display item then the actual item received on buying/selling\
    \
*   [**requirements:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#requirements)\
     - Specifies a list of requirements the player needs\
    \
*   [**ominous-strength:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#ominous-strength)\
     - Changes the strength of a ominous potion\
    \
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#premium-only-item-keys)\
\
Premium only item keys:\
\
*   [**nbtdata:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#nbt-data)\
     - highly technical data that will be applied to an item.\
    \
*   [**components:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#components)\
     \- replaces the NBTData option for 1.20.5 and newer server versions\
    \
*   [**sell-commands:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#commands)\
     \- List of commands which get executed upon selling an item.\
    \
*   [**requireItem:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#commands)\
     - Whether the shop item is required to be sold before executing a sell command.\
    \
*   [**buy-commands:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#commands)\
     \- List of commands which get executed upon purchasing an item.\
    \
*   [**giveItem:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#commands)\
     - Whether the item is given to a player after executing the buy-commands.\
    \
*   [**click-commands:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#commands)\
     - List of commands executed when the player clicks the shop item\
    \
*   [**stock-limit-global:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#global-stock)\
     - The amount of stock for the server\
    \
*   [**refill-stock:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#global-stock)\
     \- Allows the item stock limit to refill when selling items.\
    \
*   [**auto-restock-global:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#global-stock)\
     - The time to restock the global item\
    \
*   [**stock-limit-player:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#player-stock)\
     \- The amount of stock for each player individual\
    \
*   [**auto-restock-player:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#player-stock)\
     \- The time to restock the player item\
    \
*   [**sell-limit-global:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#global-sell-limit)\
     \- A selling limit for an item set server wide.\
    \
*   [**auto-restock-global-sell:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#global-sell-limit)\
     \- The time between reaching the sell limit and it restoring the original amount.\
    \
*   [**sell-limit-player:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#player-sell-limits)\
     \- A selling limit for an item set player wide.\
    \
*   [**auto-restock-player-sell:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#player-sell-limits)\
     \- The time between reaching the sell limit and it restoring the original amount.\
    \
*   [**skull-texture:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#skull-texture)\
     _\-_ Adds a custom skull texture to the player head\
    \
*   [**economy:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#economy)\
     - Allows the item to use a specific economy/currency provider\
    \
*   [**permission:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#permission)\
     - Sets a per item permission to buy/sell\
    \
*   [**permission-requirement:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#permission-requirement)\
     - Prevents the player from purchasing the item again when disabled\
    \
*   [**hideUtilLore:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#hide-util-lore)\
     \- Hides the limited item stock and limited sell lore\
    \
*   [**dynamic-pricing:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#dynamic-pricing)\
     \- Used to disable DynamicPricing per item\
    \
*   [**buy-prices:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#buy-prices)\
     - Used to add multiple payment options to a single item\
    \
*   [**sell-prices:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#sell-prices)\
     \- Used to add multiple sell prices to a single item\
    \
*   [**ignored-tags:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#ignored-tags)\
     - Used to ignore certain NBTTags for sold items\
    \
*   [**transactionMessage:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#transaction-message)\
     - Whether to send a transaction confirmation message to the player after the item has been purchased/sold from shop\
    \
*   [**display-chance:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#display-chance)\
     - Allows specific items in rotating shops to have a custom display chance\
    \
*   [**item-flags:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#item-flags)\
     - Adds various settings to the item to hide default lore\
    \
*   [**CustomModelData:**](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#custommodeldata)\
     \- Sets the CustomModelData of the item\
    \
\
If the `**displayname**` or `**name**` is empty or not set, the item will have the vanilla name.\
\
When only key `**name**` is specified and no `**displayname**` key, the item will use the name specified in the shop when you hover over it and when the item is bought.\
\
When setting the `**sell/buy**` key to any negative number, the item cannot be bought/sold in the shop. (You can also remove the buy/sell price from the item for the same effect)\
\
Creating a item with **no** buy and sell price will make it a _filler_ item which you can use to decorate your shop.\
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#breakdown)\
\
Item keys breakdown:\
\
\
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\
\
*   A simple buy/sell able shop item only needs 3 keys specified: [`**material**`](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#material)\
    , [`**buy**`](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#buy)\
     price, and [`**sell**`](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#sell)\
     price. Everything else is optional.\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      page1: # The page index\
        gui-rows: 6 # Amount in rows (1 row is 9 slots)\
        title: "   &8<=== &aExample page &c1 &8===>   "\
        items:\
          1: # The item index (can be anything, not just numbers)\
            material: milk_bucket\
            buy: 20\
            sell: 2\
      page2: # The page index\
        gui-rows: 2 # Amount in rows (1 row is 9 slots)\
        title: "   &8<=== &aExample page &c2 &8===>   " # Per page title\
        items:\
          1: # The item index (can be anything, not just numbers)\
            material: gold_ingot\
            buy: 9000\
            sell: 2800\
\
Leaving a buy/sell price unspeficied for the item will make it unbuyable/unsellable\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#material)\
\
Material:\
\
*   This is the item or block ID that will be listed/sold in the shop.\
    \
*   It MUST be a [valid name\_spaced item](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/item_id_list_pc.php)\
     for your version of Minecraft!\
    \
*   The material must be a valid item ID. Some lists to get these ID's from:\
    \
    *   [1.16 and below](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/item_id_list_pc.php)\
        \
    *   [1.18 items](https://minecraftitemids.com/)\
        \
    *   [1.19 items by CommandLeo](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1-Jf8VpmG-V2ytZ0ppAEDtVSaVYEjQ-CYAZMt-eQMNxQ/edit#gid=984941200)\
        \
    \
*   The 'Name Space' ID of an item is the code-given-name of the item.\
    \
*   It cannot have spaces or special characters and may contain underscores (\_).\
    \
*   Ex: `material: "experience_bottle"`\
    \
*   The ID is NOT case-sensitive.\
    \
*   Direct plugin compatibility: _**\*Premium feature**_\
    \
    *   ItemsAdder items: `material: "ia:<itemID>"`\
        \
    *   HeadDatabase items: `material: "hdb:<headID>"`\
        \
    *   Items from MMOItems: `material: "MMOItem:<type>.<itemID>"`\
        \
    *   Items from ExecuteableItems: `material: "ei:<itemID>"`\
        \
    *   Oraxen items: `material: "oraxen:<itemID>"`\
        \
    *   Brewery/BreweryX `material: "brewery:<brewName>.<quality>"`\
        \
    *   Nexo items: `material: "nexo:<itemID>"`\
        \
    *   Slimefun items: `material: "sf:<itemID>"`\
        \
    *   MythicMobs items: `material: "mythicmobs:<itemID>"`\
        \
    *   CraftEngine items: `material: "craftengine:<itemID>"`\
        \
    *   Items from EcoItems: `material: "ecoitems:<itemID>"`\
        \
    \
\
For compatibility reasons: any name given to items after the 1.13 'the flattening' update will work in the supported 1.8 - 1.12 versions of minecraft.\
\
You can create a dummy _spacer_ item in a shop by setting it's material to AIR (empty slot)\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#buy)\
\
Buy:\
\
*   This is the price or cost of the item that the player will have to pay to purchase or buy the item.\
    \
*   This can be any number.\
    \
*   This is the amount that will be removed or taken from the player's balance (stored in your vault-compatible economy plugin)\
    \
*   This value is only shown in the shop, and not on any bought item\
    \
\
Setting this to Any Negative Number will disable it, making it Not Purchasable/Not Buyable. Ex: `buy: -1`\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#sell)\
\
Sell:\
\
*   This is the value of the item when sold to the server.\
    \
*   This can be any number\
    \
*   This is the amount that will be given or paid to the player when the item is sold to the server (money is added to the player's balance.)\
    \
*   This value is only shown in the shop, and not on any bought item\
    \
\
Setting this to Any Negative Number will disable it, making it Not Sellable. Ex: `sell: -1`\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#name)\
\
Name:\
\
*   This will specify a name for the item when it is bought from shop AND when no `displayname` option is specified it will also be the name for the item when hovering over it in shop.\
    \
*   It may contain [Chat-Codes](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/color_list_pc.php)\
     [(Color/Formatting)](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/color_list_pc.php)\
     or [RGB colors](https://colorspire.com/rgb-color-wheel/)\
    .\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    #Example item with a name that is only shown in the shop, AND a name that is on the item bought.\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: milk_bucket\
            buy: 20\
            sell: 2\
            displayname: "&f&lGot Milk?" #this is what is shown in the shop.\
            name: "&bWe got &f&lMilk!" #this is the name that will be on the item when purchased/bought.\
\
Only specifing option `**name**` on the item will make it use the same displayname when hovering over it AND the name for the item when it is bought.\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#display-name)\
\
Displayname:\
\
*   Do not confuse this option with `name` since this option will ONLY set the name for the display item inside the shop(When hovering over the item)\
    \
*   It will NOT be on the item when purchased/bought.\
    \
*   It may contain [Chat-Codes](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/color_list_pc.php)\
     [(Color/Formatting)](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/color_list_pc.php)\
     or [RGB colors](https://colorspire.com/rgb-color-wheel/)\
    .\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    #Example item with a display name that is only shown in the shop, and not on the item bought\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: milk_bucket\
            buy: 20\
            sell: 2\
            displayname: "Got Milk?"\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#lore)\
\
Lore:\
\
*   Create custom text and info about the item!\
    \
*   It may contain [Chat-Codes](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/color_list_pc.php)\
     [(Color/Formatting)](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/color_list_pc.php)\
     or [RGB colors](https://colorspire.com/rgb-color-wheel/)\
    .\
    \
*   You may use placeholder `%buyPrice%/%sellPrice%`\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    #Example item with a name that is only shown in the shop, AND a name that is on the item bought.\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: netherite_shovel\
            buy: 2000000\
            sell: 5000\
            displayname: "&c&lDevil's Paw"\
            name: "&c&lDevil's Paw"\
            lore:\
            - "&5This is the severed hand of"\
            - "&5the devil himself. Be careful,"\
            - "&5who can say what unholy powers"\
            - "&5it may still contain..."\
\
The `**lore/displaylore**` key work the same as the `**name/displayname**` key but instead it specifies the lore. Meaning that when only `**lore**` is specified, the item will use the lore as the lore when hovering over the item AND when you buy the item.\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#displaylore)\
\
Displaylore:\
\
*   Do not confuse this option with `lore` since this option will ONLY set the lore for the display item inside the shop(When hovering over the item)\
    \
*   Create custom text and info about the item!\
    \
*   It may contain [Chat-Codes](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/color_list_pc.php)\
     [(Color/Formatting)](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/color_list_pc.php)\
     or [RGB colors](https://colorspire.com/rgb-color-wheel/)\
    .\
    \
*   You may use placeholder `%buyPrice%/%sellPrice%`\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: AMETHYST_SHARD\
            buy: 10\
            sell: 5\
            lore: # This is the lore of the item when bought from shop\
            - '&cNotch'\
            displaylore: # This is the lore of the item when hovering over it in shop\
            - '&1Gypopo'\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#hidepricinglore)\
\
HidePricingLore:\
\
*   Option `**hidePricingLore**` will do what the name suggests, it will hide the default pricing lore of the item so you could add your own for example\
    \
*   This will hide the pricing lore even if the item is still purchase/sell-able\
    \
*   This option comes in handy when you want to make _dummy/display_ items\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      page1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: LAVA_BUCKET\
            buy: 200\
            sell: 75\
            hidePricingLore: true # This will make the prices not visible for the player\
          2:\
            material: WATER_BUCKET\
            buy: -1\
            sell: -1\
            hidePricingLore: true # This will hide the default 'This item cannot be bought/sold' lore\
\
This option allows to hide the default pricing lore as a **per item** setting but to fast forward it you can empty out the lore inside the [language file](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/languages#language-file-example)\
 which will do the same but for **every** item\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#hidedecorationlore)\
\
HideDecorationLore:\
\
*   The `**hideDecorationLore**` will hide the usage/decoration lore per item\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      page6:\
        items:\
          clean_item:\
            material: TOTEM_OF_UNDYING\
            buy: 7500\
            sell: 725\
            hidePricingLore: true\
            hideDecorationLore: true\
            displaylore:\
            - "&aComes with a heavy investment of just &f7500$"\
            - "&abut can save lives when on hand, which is worth it if you ask me."\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#slot)\
\
Slot:\
\
*   Option `**slot**` determines the position of the item inside the shop page\
    \
*   **TIP**: It is possible to display one item at multiple positions by specifying multiple slots\
    \
    *   Example: `slot: 1-9,36-45` which will display the same item at all slots from 1 thru 9 and 36 thru 45\
        \
    *   Example: `slot: 20,24-28,30,31` which will display the same item at slot 20, all slots from 24 thru 28, slot 30 and 31\
        \
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        gui-rows: 6\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: chainmail_chestplate\
            buy: 25\
            sell: 10\
            name: "&d&lKnight's armor piece"\
            slot: 11\
          2:\
            material: iron_chestplate\
            buy: 35\
            sell: 15\
            name: "&d&lKnight's armor piece"\
            slot: 13\
          3:\
            material: diamond_chestplate\
            buy: 50\
            name: "&d&lKnight's armor piece"\
            slot: 15\
          4:\
            material: netherite_chestplate\
            buy: 100\
            name: "&d&lKnight's armor piece"\
            slot: 17\
          999:\
            material: LIGHT_BLUE_STAINED_GLASS_PANE\
            name: '&bFill item'\
            slot: 1-10,18,19,27,28,36,37,38-45\
\
The slot of items need to be in range of the shop page size, if not, the item will not be able to load with a error in console.\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#stack-size)\
\
Stack size:\
\
*   Option `**stack-size**` sets the stack size of the shop item\
    \
*   When for example the stack size is set to 5, when the player purchases 2 stacks of this item, they will receive 10 items in total\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: APPLE\
            name: "&cA stack of 20 apples"\
            buy: 200\
            sell: 50\
            stack-size: 20\
\
**Note:** When setting a items stack-size, the prices of the item count for the whole stack. So meaning with the item above, 10 apples would be worth $100 and sell for $25.\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#enchantment-glint)\
\
Enchantment glint:\
\
*   This option lets u add a enchantment glow effect to any item to give your shop items a more personal touch.\
    \
\
**Note**: This will add a 'dummy' enchantment of aqua affinity 1 to the item, but default lore will be removed.\
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1: \
        items:\
          1:\
            material: BLAZE_ROD\
            name: "&cShiny rod"\
            buy: 50.0\
            sell: 10.0\
            enchantment-glint: true\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#enchantments)\
\
Enchantments:\
\
*   Add as many enchantments as you want to an item!\
    \
*   `enchantments` is a yml-list-format list of [valid enchantments](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/enchantment_list_pc.php)\
     that are applied to the item when bought.\
    \
*   Enchantments must be in this format: `<Enchantment>:<level>` (without the "<>") if no level is specified (no `:1`, it will be level 1)\
    \
*   Enchantments [must be valid/exist in your version of MC.](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/enchantment_list_pc.php)\
    \
*   To enable enchants greater than default/vanilla you must enable `allow-unsafe-enchants: true` in the [config.yml](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/config.yml#allow-unsafe-enchants)\
    \
*   Custom enchants from external plugins like EcoEnchants, AdvancedEnchantments, ExcelentEnchants are directly supported using the format of `<plugin>:<enchantment>:<level>` _\*Premium feature_\
    \
*   You can find [a list of enchantments for your version of MC here](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/enchantment_list_pc.php)\
    !\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    #Example of an Enchanted item:\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: diamond_pickaxe\
            buy: 2000000\
            sell: 5000\
            displayname: "&4Silky Smooth"\
            name: "&4Silky Smooth"\
            lore:\
            - "&5The smooooothest pick!"\
            enchantments:\
            - "silk_touch:1"\
            - "efficiency:5"\
            - "ecoenchants:blast_mining:3" # Example of a custom enchant from EcoEnchants\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#potion-types)\
\
Potion Types:\
\
*   Add as many potion-effects to Potions and Tipped Arrows as you want!\
    \
*   `potiontypes` is a yml-list-format list of [valid potion types](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#potion-types-table)\
     that are applied to the item when bought.\
    \
*   Potion Types must be [valid vanilla potion types for your version of Minecraft](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#potion-types-table)\
    \
*   Valid [materials](https://www.digminecraft.com/lists/item_id_list_pc.php)\
     that these effects can be applied to are: `potion`, `splash_potion`, `lingering_potion`, and `tipped_arrow`.\
    \
\

#### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#potions-examples)\
\
Potions Examples:\
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            #a common craftable vanilla potion:\
            material: POTION\
            displayname: "Potion of Fire Resistance"\
            buy: 11.9\
            sell: 2.98\
            potiontypes:\
            - fire_resistance\
          2: \
            #example of 'custom' potion: full list NOT Reccomended for survival servers!!\
            material: POTION\
            displayname: "&bSuperman Potion"\
            name: "&bSuperman Potion"\
            buy: 5000\
            sell: 50\
            potiontypes:\
            - long_fire_resistance\
            - long_night_vision\
            - long_leaping\
            - long_regeneration\
            - long_strength\
            - long_swiftness\
            - long_water_breathing\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#spawner-type)\
\
Spawner Type:\
\
*   `spawnertype` must be a [valid Name\_spaced mob for your version of minecraft.](https://www.digminecraft.com/mobs/index.php)\
    \
*   [All entity types that can be used on spawners can be found here](https://www.digminecraft.com/mobs/index.php)\
    .\
    \
*   **All** `**spawner**` **material items REQUIRE this setting** to correctly apply the mob-type when placed (\*With the exception of 3rd party plugins where you have configured [NBT-data](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#nbt-data)\
     on the item. \*Premium feature)\
    \
*   NOTE: this setting is only works if you have [spawner-break](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/config.yml#spawner-settings)\
     and [spawner-break](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/config.yml#spawner-settings)\
     enabled in the [config.yml](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/config.yml)\
    \
\
**Tip**: When key `**name**` has been specified on the item, the spawner will have the specified name when mined by a player! :)\
\
Copy\
\
    #Example Spawner item\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: SPAWNER\
            #you MUST specify a spawner type, otherwise they will always be pig(default) spawners\
            spawnertype: BLAZE\
            #the 'name' will also be applied to the item when MINED if the mined spawner's mobtype is specified in ESGUI (and spawner-break is enabled in in config)\
            #the name is optional, however without it, you can't tell what mob the spawner is set too without showing nbt data on your client (it will just say 'spawner' to everyone)\
            name: '&6&lBlaze &fSpawner'\
            buy: 125000\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#recipe)\
\
Recipes:\
\
*   A list of recipes that can be applied to the item and given to the player when the item is used.\
    \
*   Recipe books will give/learn the recipes for a player when they activate it(right click the book).\
    \
\
We will not be going in depth into recipes here. [Please consult knowledge\_book documentation here.](https://minecraft.fandom.com/wiki/Recipe_book)\
 However, the majority of recipes are written as `minecraft:iron_ingot` for example.\
\
Copy\
\
    #Example Knowledge Book item:\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: Knowledge_book\
            name: "Get Rusty"\
            recipes: \
            - "minecraft:iron_ingot"\
            - "minecraft:furnace"\
            - "minecraft:NETHERITE_SWORD"\
            buy: 10\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#skull-owner)\
\
Skull Owner:\
\
*   `skullowner` must be a valid mojang-account player's name.\
    \
*   If the playername is invalid/does not exist, the default/generic texture will be used.\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    #Example Playerhead item:\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: player_head\
            skullowner: notch\
            buy: 500\
            sell: 50\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#armor-color)\
\
Armor Color:\
\
*   `armorcolor` must be in a valid hexadecimal format. _**Example: '0x00FF00', '#00FF00' or '00FF00'**_\
    \
*   See this site for a color wheel you can use: [https://www.colorspire.com/rgb-color-wheel/](https://www.colorspire.com/rgb-color-wheel/)\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    #Example ArmorColor item:\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: player_head\
            armorcolor: "0x00FF00"\
            buy: 500\
            sell: 50\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#firework-options)\
\
Firework options:\
\
*   `**duration:**` is the flight duration of the firework\
    \
    *   Valid options: `**1**`, `**2**`, `**3**` (Each value represents how much gunpowder would be used)\
        \
    \
*   `**colors:**` a list of colors that are used inside the firework's main exploisen\
    \
    *   Valid options are: `**White**`, `**Orange**`, `**Magenta**`, `**Light_Blue**`, `**Yellow**`, `**Lime**`, `**Pink**`, `**Gray**`, `**Light_Gray**`, `**Cyan**`, `**Purple**`, `**Blue**`, `**Brown**`, `**Green**`, `**Red**`, `**Black**`\
        \
    \
*   `**fade-colors:**` a list of colors that are used inside the firework's fading\
    \
    *   Valid options: `**White**`, `**Orange**`, `**Magenta**`, `**Light_Blue**`, `**Yellow**`, `**Lime**`, `**Pink**`, `**Gray**`, `**Light_Gray**`, `**Cyan**`, `**Purple**`, `**Blue**`, `**Brown**`, `**Green**`, `**Red**`, `**Black**`\
        \
    \
*   `**flicker: true/false**` Whether or not this firework has the twinkle effect, this is the same as using glowstone when crafting\
    \
*   `**trail: true/false**` Whether or not this explosion has the trail effect, this is the same as using a diamond when crafting\
    \
*   `**shape:**` The shape of the explosion of the firework\
    \
    *   Valid options: `**ball**`, `**ball_large**`, `**star**`, `**burst**`, `**creeper**`\
        \
    \
\
If you want to add fade-colors, flicker, trail or shape you need to specify atleast one color\
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          1:\
            material: FIREWORK\
            buy: 38.50\
            sell: 20\
            duration: 2\
            colors:\
              - "cyan"\
              - "purple"\
            fade-colors:\
              - "black"\
              - "gray"\
            flicker: true\
            trail: true\
            shape: BURST\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#instrument)\
\
Instrument:\
\
*   Add this to goat horns to specify which sound they create\
    \
    *   Valid sounds: `**PONDER**`, `**SING**`, `**SEEK**`, `**FEEL**`, `**ADMIRE**`, `**CALL**`, `**YEARN**`, `**DREAM**`\
        \
    \
*   The item material needs to be a GOAT\_HORN for this option to work\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          19:  \
            material: GOAT_HORN\
            buy: 100  \
            sell: 25  \
            instrument: "dream"\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#sub-sections)\
\
Sub sections:\
\
*   This item option will link the item to a shop section\
    \
    *   Upon clicking the item the player will enter the section linked\
        \
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          29:\
            material: "COBBLESTONE"\
            section: Cobblestones\
            lore:\
            - "&6&lClick to enter the CobbleStone section"\
\
### \
\
[](https://wiki.gpplugins.com/economyshopgui/file-configuration/shops.yml#stew-effect)\
\
Stew effect:\
\
*   Allows you to specify a potion effect on a suspicious stew\
    \
\
Copy\
\
    pages:\
      pages1:\
        items:\
          Stew_1:\
            material: SUSPICIOUS_STEW\
            buy: 5\
            sell: 2\
            stew-effect: REGENERATION\
\
